Some devices support sleep/hibernate modes where the device (PC, etc) can be woken by a so-called magic packet on the ethernet (or wireless) interface. This tool can send this magic packet. This tool only sends the magic packet. Putting a device in sleep where it can be woken has to be configured \"manually\".
